  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_c0f775e6-3650-44fa-9628-a638d2d99462'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

  <span id="freeText5526987398705053751" style="display:none"><i>“My life was complete. Happy, content, everything neat and perfect.<br />Then it all changed.<br />I was sold.”</i><br /><br />Tess Snow has everything she ever wanted: one more semester before a career in property development, a loving boyfriend, and a future dazzling bright with possibility. <br /><br />For their two year anniversary, Brax surprises Tess with a romantic trip to Mexico. Sandy beaches, delicious cocktails, and soul-connecting sex set the mood for a wonderful holiday. With a full heart, and looking forward to a passion filled week, Tess is on top of the world.<br /><br />But lusty paradise is shattered.<br /><br />Kidnapped. Drugged. Stolen. Tess is forced into a world full of darkness and terror. <br /><br />Captive and alone with no savior, no lover, no faith, no future, Tess evolves from terrified girl to fierce fighter. But no matter her strength, it can’t save her from the horror of being sold.<br /><br />Can Brax find Tess before she’s broken and ruined, or will Tess’s new owner change her life forever?<br /><br /><i>A New Adult Dark Contemporary Romance, not suitable for people sensitive to grief, slavery, and nonconsensual sex. A story about finding love in the strangest of places, a will of iron that grows from necessity, and forgiveness that may not be enough.</i></span>

<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/22216466-jessica"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1406319423i/22216466._UY100_CR3,0,100,100_.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/22216466-jessica">Jessica</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">I have read both this and Captive in the Dark series, but I can honestly say you'll get more first person brutality from this series. The first book i<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">I have read both this and Captive in the Dark series, but I can honestly say you'll get more first person brutality from this series. The first book is a bit rough around the edges (meaning how it was written, lacks much needed editing), but the plot is good and gets better throughout the series. It's not for everyone by any stretch of the imagination. It's dark, not like sexy bondage dark, but kidnapping, rape and torture dark (and some sexy bondage dark too). And 'Tears' it's less about revenge and more about the characters healing, I personally don't associate the two series but I can see how some people would. <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>

<div id="review_669071084" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/669071084" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/669071084?book_show_action=true">Jul 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer669071084" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11102938274891844858"><b>5 sparrow stars</b><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/8720e6e3-88d8-4d0d-bff9-624fdf7144b8_zps7f124a01.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429387i/860117.jpg' alt=' photo 8720e6e3-88d8-4d0d-bff9-624fdf7144b8_zps7f124a01.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Tess Snow is a twenty year old college student who lives with her boyfriend, Brax, in Austarila. Brax and Tess have a good relationship. It’s sweet, simple, easy. <br/><b>
  <blockquote>Brax wanted me. Brax was safe. I loved him in my own way.</blockquote>
</b><br/>Brax is everything Tess could ever want in a boyfriend. Everything with them is perfect. Except their sex life. Tess has always had different wants and needs than her boyfriend. She wants to try to step out of the box with Brax, and what better time to do t</span>
  <span id="freeText11102938274891844858" style="display:none"><b>5 sparrow stars</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/8720e6e3-88d8-4d0d-bff9-624fdf7144b8_zps7f124a01.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429387i/860117.jpg" alt=" photo 8720e6e3-88d8-4d0d-bff9-624fdf7144b8_zps7f124a01.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Tess Snow is a twenty year old college student who lives with her boyfriend, Brax, in Austarila. Brax and Tess have a good relationship. It’s sweet, simple, easy. <br><b>
  <blockquote>Brax wanted me. Brax was safe. I loved him in my own way.</blockquote>
</b><br>Brax is everything Tess could ever want in a boyfriend. Everything with them is perfect. Except their sex life. Tess has always had different wants and needs than her boyfriend. She wants to try to step out of the box with Brax, and what better time to do that then on their vacation to Cancun? <br><br>While on vacation, the unthinkable happens to Tess. She is taken. Stolen. Kidnapped to be sold. Tess tries to find ways to escape, get out, but she is unsuccessful. She doesn’t make it easy on the kidnappers, she fights. <br><b>
  <blockquote>I would never give up. I would fight until I died.</blockquote>
</b> After being held into captivity for a while, she finds out she is leaving Mexico, going to an undisclosed location. She is going to her master. This terrifies her more than anything. <br><i>
  <blockquote>Three little words. If anyone asked what I was most afraid of, what terrified me, stole my breath, and made my life flicker before my eyes, I would say three little words. <br><b>I was sold.</b>
</blockquote>
</i><br>When Tess gets to her new home, she is surprised. It is big and beautiful. She meets her new master. His name is Q. She doesn’t know much about Q. All she knows is he is French, rich, handsome, and he owns her. That makes him a monster in her eyes. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/02904496-2cef-41da-8f45-c1ecc4ece414_zps5b510434.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429387i/860118.jpg" alt=" photo 02904496-2cef-41da-8f45-c1ecc4ece414_zps5b510434.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Even though she knows these things about Q, there is something about him that excites her. She hates how she responds to him. She feels something for him that she’s never felt before. All those things she has always wanted and tried to hide... thats no longer possible. <br><b>
  <blockquote>I hated him, knew what he did was wrong, but my body, shit, my body didn’t care.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Q has some dark desires, but he’s not the typical dark and sadistic master. You can tell throughout the story he goes back and forth trying to keep his wants and desires in check. He doesn’t want to go to far, but Tess has her own wants and desires. She has a way of pushing Q, bringing out the side of him he tries to cage. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/f57be16f-5eed-4283-84e4-1c64d1fa6c4b_zpsb6b097a9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429387i/860119.jpg" alt=" photo f57be16f-5eed-4283-84e4-1c64d1fa6c4b_zpsb6b097a9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>‘Come for me, esclave.’</b><br><br>  How far is too far? Tess is a strong character. She is not easily broken. She will do anything for her freedom. But she’s fighting a battle. A battle between her mind and her body. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/e0bf06b9-9bc3-46cc-9c65-d845bbe0039d_zps6d8f32fb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429387i/860120.jpg" alt=" photo e0bf06b9-9bc3-46cc-9c65-d845bbe0039d_zps6d8f32fb.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <blockquote>“After tonight, every time I say your name you’ll get wet for me. I not only own your body but your identity, too. Do you deny it?” <br>“No, I don’t deny it. I’m yours. Through and through.”</blockquote>
</i> She starts to feel things she never imagined she would feel while in captivity. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>‘Monsters find each other in the dark.’<br><br>I’d never felt this way. This uninhibited. This free.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/a80b8937-1d0b-4b22-895f-c00f4a638656_zpsa81bcb07.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429387i/860121.jpg" alt=" photo a80b8937-1d0b-4b22-895f-c00f4a638656_zpsa81bcb07.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>I finally found a place where my twistedness belonged. In Q’s arms.<br><br>‘He opened my cage and allowed me to fly. I can’t stop it if my freedom is here.’</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br>Q and Tess...There is so much I want to say about Q’s character, but I don’t want to spoil any of the book. There were a few things about him I assumed, but also a few things about him that surprised me. I love a good damaged man, so you know I loved Q. He was just irresistible. And the french... I could just imagine his accent and it made me melt. Tess was tough. She was resilient. She knew what she wanted, and she went after it. I respected her for that. I loved Q and Tess separately, but I loved them more together. <br><i>
  <blockquote>‘Je suis à toi’. <b>I am yours.</b><br>‘Nous sommes les uns des autres.’ <b>We are each others.</b>
</blockquote>
</i><br>This was a fantastic read. It captivated me from the beginning and I couldn’t put it down. We read this story from Tess’s perspective, but we get a nice epilogue from Q’s p.o.v. Beautiful. Emotional. Conflicting. Sexy. Edgy. All those things and more. <br><br>I was expecting this to be a little darker and more disturbing. It had it’s dark moments, but it wasn’t as much of a mindfuck as I expected it to be. It didn’t make me enjoy it any less. For those of you that don’t love the dark and disturbing reads, it will probably be on the dark side for you. There were a few scenes that were on the dark and twisted side, but not as many as I was expecting. Overall, I was very impressed with this debut novel. A 5 star read for me and going on my favorites shelf! Anyone looking for a semi-dark, unconventional love story with some bdsm, give it a go! I am looking forward to reading more from this author in the future! <br><br><br><i>**ARC kindly provided by author, Pepper Winters, in an exchange for an honest review.**</i></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer875730019" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12816077841214421248">This is was the first Pepper Winters' book that I read, and I have no regrets. None at all. <br/>After reading this book , I'd found my favorite author. <br/>Everything Pepper Winters writes, I will read it because I know that it won't be disappointing. <br/>This book is one of my unforgettable reads. It is that good. <br/>I should say this before I review this book that it's a Dark Contemporary Romance, not suitable for people sensitive to grief, slavery and non consensual sex. <br/><br/>Tears of Tess is about 20 year old T</span>
  <span id="freeText12816077841214421248" style="display:none">This is was the first Pepper Winters' book that I read, and I have no regrets. None at all. <br />After reading this book , I'd found my favorite author. <br />Everything Pepper Winters writes, I will read it because I know that it won't be disappointing. <br />This book is one of my unforgettable reads. It is that good. <br />I should say this before I review this book that it's a Dark Contemporary Romance, not suitable for people sensitive to grief, slavery and non consensual sex. <br /><br />Tears of Tess is about 20 year old Tess Snow who lives with her boyfriend Brax. <br />Their relationship is good and sweet, but even though Brax means absolutely everything to Tess, their sex life isn't as good.<br />So while on vacation with each other, Tess gets unexpectedly kidnapped. <br />She is taken from Brax and sold. <br />Tess does everything she can to escape her kidnappers, but she always fails. <br />That doesn't stop her from fighting her kidnappers for freedom, but even though she tries at every opportunity, she's always unsuccessful. <br />Tess gets held in captivity for awhile, but then she later finds out that she's leaving for Mexico to meet her new Master.<br />When Tess goes to her new home, she's amazed more than anything. <br />Her new home is beautiful. <br />Her new master's name is Q. <br />He's French, handsome and rich.<br />He also owns Tess completely. <br /><br />I first read this book ages ago, and I've read it again a few times because I adore this book. <br />I'm still confused as to why I haven't reviewed this book before, because it should've been on the top of my to do list. <br />I'm going to have reread this book anyways, because I need to read the 3rd book to which I haven't read yet!<br />I'm telling you, trying to fit in writing and do a little bit of reading in the same day, is tricky. <br />I wish the days were longer. <br />I'm finding that reviewing books is kind of fun actually.<br />As you can tell I haven't stopped reviewing books for the last 2/3 days.<br />It makes you think though, and that's a good thing in my case. <br />It's weird giving my personal opinion about something, because I'm one of those people that keep my opinions to myself, so to share my opinions with you is a good feeling, a feeling I'm not entirely used to. Yet. <br />Back to the book, I don't think I've read a BDSM/Dark book that tops Tears of Tess. <br />Maybe I haven't read a book like that yet, so I'm always open to books with a Dark vibe in it. <br />It's really strange because I'm always drawn to books with the genre Dark in it, and I don't know if that should be worrying or not, but books like that tend to be on my favorites list more than any other genre! xD<br />But saying that, Tears of Tess is one of those books I just want to treasure for the rest of my life. <br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

On a daytrip sightseeing on a motorbike <b>Tess is kidnapped</b>, leaving Brax for dead and her future in jeopardy. After a gruesome time in captivity, abused, starved, mishandled and violated on many levels she is <b>sold and hand delivered to her new master, Q aka Quincy Mercer</b>, a wealthy Frenchman living in a chateau somewhere in France. But Tess has <b>no interest is submitting</b> nor accepting her new master and puts up a fight.<br><br>Their attraction is palpable putting both their lives in tailspins and their <b>sexual desires under scrutiny</b>. Tess doesn’t want to like Q, yet she desires him. Q is hot-cold and an enigma. He warns her of the monster inside of him, which will unfold with story. But rest assure, not everything is as it seems. <b>This is Tess journey of sexual exploration and growth under the backdrop of her captivity by Q</b>.<br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIFS%20for%20my%20reads/ToT1HxBSbysb_zps6b15a3a1.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

I am very <b>happy were it left Tess and Q</b>. That said, I am both curious AND nervous where book 2, <b>

  <span id="freeText15064655774814215213" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <u>Triggers</u>

  <b><br><br>*Rape<br>*Attempt to Rape<br>*Non-consensual sexual act<br>*Physical abuse and Violence</b>
</blockquote><br><br><br>♤<b>5▪Dark▪ Fairytale▪ Stars</b>♤<br><br><br><br>Before starting my review I need to say this - <br><br>This book really opened my senses freed my thought process <br><br>And Girl, just because a man touches you without your consent that doesn’t make you filthy he Didn't degrade you he degraded Himself <br><br>I hope and pray all the rapist all the sinners burn in hell <br><br><b>"Your Lady Part Doesn’t Define You"</b><br><br><br><blockquote>******<b>THE REVIEW</b>******</blockquote><br><br>First things first this book is not for everyone you have to keep your mind open to read it<br><br>You will have to Think as Tess <br>Imagine yourself in Tess's position to understand her, all her actions, her and Q's relationship. <br><br><br><br><b>Tess Snow</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"She was	warrior	who’d	seen	blood,	stared	monsters	in	the	face,<br>and	knew	without	a	doubt	her	life	would	be	hers	again."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1603546740i/30282421._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Tess taught me how to fight back in every situation. It is important to never give up on <b>YOURSELF</b>.<br>and it is not just about her being kidnapped and all those incidents she had to go through. It's about her whole life, she had to fight for everything relentlessly.<br><br>Again It's not about just surviving or passing another day It's about <b>Living</b><br>She is someone who could break but not bend.<br>She is one of the most fierce female protagonists I came across. I don't know how I would have kept my sanity if I was her.<br>She is Actually a True Warrior in Every Sense.<br><br><br><br><b>Q</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"No	one	touched	me	so	tenderly.	Never	had	my	parents cuddled	or	offered	comfort	in	their	arms.	I	grew	up	never knowing	how	to	hug	or	kiss	or	love."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1603546740i/30282422._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>People will call Q erotic but the minute I meet Q I felt him as a protective figure, someone with whom you feel safe.<br>My sixth sense was telling me this man isn't wrong. He can't be wrong. <br><br>I loved how Q took care of Tess after that horrific incident. I loved how didn’t treat her like a <b>broken doll</b> after those pricks took her without her consent (I can't even use the "R" word again it hurts too much)<br><br><b>He is the Dark Knight</b><br><br><br><u>Special Mention</u><br><br><b>Brax</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“The	truth	hurts	less	than	fibs	and fakers.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br>First of all, I wholeheartedly apologise that I called Brax <b>Vanilla</b><br><br>It's not about a man being <b>Vanilla or Choclate</b><br><br>It's about how you treat your girl <br>and Brax treats his girl beautifully.<br><br><b>But the question is Do you want to live with a man who doesn't make you feel safe ?</b> <br>My Answer is NO! <br><br>We girls feel protected with our father right? I think we seek the same level of comfort and protectiveness in our respective husband or boyfriend.<br>It's not about your man being muscular or adventurous<br>It is about this feeling that he will fight for you with everything he had not just with goons but in every circumstance.<br>May be another girl will find this protectiveness with Brax, but he was not the right cut for Tess, and even if Tess didn't meet Q, Brax would not be the ultimate man for Tess.<br><br><br><br><b>My Ethics</b><br><br>I strictly keep my mind open whenever I read any dark romance. I did the same thing here.<br>I always imagine myself as the female protagonist whenever read a book.<br>So as Tess I would live and love Q and embrace his life and Taste.<br><br>But As ME Nope! <br>I don't think so I could come back to a place which haunted me.<br>That pain would be too much to bear.<br>Maybe I would convince Q to live somewhere else more vibrant and I would try to tame him.<br>If you see as a reader you will find that he had some deep issues, and Q's is fighting his demon and Tess is sort of feeding him.<br><br>Anyway there are two more books I hope they will figure out there problems and slove it like a fighter they are 🖤<br><br>and hopefully<br><br><b>LOVE WILL DEFEAT THOSE MONSTERS IN THE DARK</b><br><br>Happy Reading 🖤🖤</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer673234579" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12955958758328564618"><a href='http://imgur.com/a2cmJ5b' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429981i/861813.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>6 Captivating Stars!!!!!!!!!!!!<br/><br/>Words CAN.NOT describe what a beautiful, emotional, gut-wrenching, soul-searching kind of read Tears of Tess was for me.<br/><br/>I simply LOVED it!<br/><br/>My emotions through-out</b><br/><br/>At 1% when I read <br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>I wanted a new label. One that said: girlfriend who will do anything to be tied, spanked, and fucked all over rather than adored</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> <br/><br/>I just knew I was going into something special. <br/><br/>At 11% I was like OH SHIT!<br/><br/>At 30 % I had a big smile on my face<br/><br/>At 46 % I was just a BALL. OF. EMOT</span>
  <span id="freeText12955958758328564618" style="display:none"><a href="http://imgur.com/a2cmJ5b" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429981i/861813.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>6 Captivating Stars!!!!!!!!!!!!<br><br>Words CAN.NOT describe what a beautiful, emotional, gut-wrenching, soul-searching kind of read Tears of Tess was for me.<br><br>I simply LOVED it!<br><br>My emotions through-out</b><br><br>At 1% when I read <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>I wanted a new label. One that said: girlfriend who will do anything to be tied, spanked, and fucked all over rather than adored</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> <br><br>I just knew I was going into something special. <br><br>At 11% I was like OH SHIT!<br><br>At 30 % I had a big smile on my face<br><br>At 46 % I was just a BALL. OF. EMOTIONS!!!<br><br>At 68% I couldn’t tear away from my tablet, it was just so good.<br><br>At 86% my heart was beating a million miles<br><br><b>
  <u>At 100% I just had a book orgasm.</u>
</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/O7qfHF7" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429981i/861814.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>[Summary]</b><br><br>Tess is an ordinary girl from Australia, with an ordinary boyfriend and an ordinary sex-life. But she wants more than the ordinary sex-life… something less conventional. Tess and her boyfriend go on Holiday to Cancun Mexico and all is well until she gets kidnapped and sold to a man who goes by the name of Q. Q is no ordinary Master. He’s no ordinary man and Tess has become his new Slave. <br><br><b>[Disclaimer]</b><br><br>Let’s put that disclaimer out there, because I will get asked this A LOT. First off, I wasn’t a fan of Captive and not because it was too dark. I couldn’t find any redeeming qualities in Caleb. So if you want to compare Tears of Tess to Captive, please do not. It’s not the same. Tears of Tess has its own unique writing style and plot. However, Tears of Tess does have the same feel as Captive, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/543196572" rel="nofollow noopener">Consequences</a>, and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/639161773" rel="nofollow noopener">Killing Sarai</a>. Hopefully that makes sense. <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/byx2tF8" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429981i/861815._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>I hadn’t gone Stockholmy- I hated him, knew what he did was wrong, but my body, shit, my body didn’t care.<br><br>He would look after me as long as I pleased him</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><b>[Tess]</b><br><br>Tess is wonderful, she smart, strong, resilient, beautiful and the fact she is Australian just tickles me to no end. Tears of Tess is written from her POV and you completely, 100% FEEL FOR HER. I got her emotions, I got her struggles and yes at some times, I was gutted with shock and grief, but I wouldn’t have it any other way. I loved her.<br><br><b>[Q]</b> <br><br>Oh God. Q. I think that is my new favorite letter. I LOVED Q. I want to make babies with Q, I want him to use me, abuse me and do it all over again. Could Pepper have written a more perfectly, beautifully damaged character? I think not. <b>Q was P.E.R.F.E.C.T.</b> I saw the wealthy, controlled alpha male. I also saw the tortured and vulnerable monster. Q had such conflictions which rounded his character nicely. <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/6SbwQVN" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429981i/861816.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Q moved with power and undeniable knowledge of perfect control.<br><br>I will learn who you are one day. That is a promise. And my promises are law</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><b>[Review]</b><br><br>The beginning starts out with a lot of character development on Tess’ part. You really get to know Tess and if you are like me, I love character development. I really got to know her and her issues. When Tess got kidnapped, I felt like I was jolted into a crazy ride and I loved it. It would not say Tears of Tess was a difficult read, I would say it was a dark read. <br><br>I love the power struggle between Tess and Q. Even though Q had all of the power, the chemistry between the Hero and Heroine just worked for me. The main reason why I love this book so much is because I understood Q. Even when he was sadistic, mean, and just didn’t seem to give a fuck, I got him and I loved him even more for it. <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/SOMT7oJ" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429981i/861817._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Only think of me and what I’m doing. There is intimacy in pain esclave. Let me make your pain my pleasure.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>And the steam…. Yes they were my favorite parts. Let me clarify, I love steam, but kinky, very different and pushing the boundaries steam, well damn. I LOVE IT! Pepper did not disappoint. If you want something different, you will get it.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/vlumDO4" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429981i/861818._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>…put a man who wanted to hurt in front of me, with fucking on his mind and bondage in his thoughts, and I unraveled like the slut I’d become.<br><br>The monster roared, beating his cheats, salivating at the thought of what was to come.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Pepper is an excellent writer and I am completely shocked she wrote Tears of Tess in seven weeks. That’s pure fucking talent. I’ve said it before and I say it again. <b>Reading books like Tears of Tess is the sole reason why I do what I do. It’s the reason why I pick up a book, write about it and let the world know, because when you write something that it just so beyond perfect, beautiful and good, EVERYONE should know.</b><br><br><i>An ARC was provided by the author in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br>To read the prologue and it's good, visit, <a href="http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com/2013/08/book-review-tears-of-tess-by-pepper.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Jacqueline's Reads</a>I</span>
  <a data-text-id="12955958758328564618" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_668978826" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/668978826" />
    <a title="Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie"><img alt="Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505392311p2/11641363.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/668978826?book_show_action=true">Jul 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie " href="/user/show/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie">Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=kidnap-or-abduction">kidnap-or-abduction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=arc-or-netgalley">arc-or-netgalley</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer668978826" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16107125711067151107"><b>Actual rating: 2.5 Stars</b><br/><br/>It pains me to give this book anything below 4 stars, I really had high hopes when I started reading this book. The prologue was intriguing and for about 22% I was really enjoying the direction and pace of the story. But after that the story started losing it's allure for me, the captor wasn't what I expected. There is a very delicate balance when you are writing a captivity story, you have your two roles: Captive and Captor. When the line between the two starts to blur, </span>
  <span id="freeText16107125711067151107" style="display:none"><b>Actual rating: 2.5 Stars</b><br><br>It pains me to give this book anything below 4 stars, I really had high hopes when I started reading this book. The prologue was intriguing and for about 22% I was really enjoying the direction and pace of the story. But after that the story started losing it's allure for me, the captor wasn't what I expected. There is a very delicate balance when you are writing a captivity story, you have your two roles: Captive and Captor. When the line between the two starts to blur, you've lost me.<br><br>But I kept reading, hoping that it would get better. But unfortunately not. I guess the story was too predictable for me, in my opinion this story was a case of the characters had sadistic cravings or urges and couldn't accept this part of themselves. This is angst not dark. And when it comes to non-consent, I only know of one incident where non-consensual-sex occurred, the rest was just reluctance.<br><br>I am a huge fan of anti-heroes and have read many books with this type of character. The one thing that makes or brakes the book is an anti-hero who feels remorse too early in the story. Once again the story holds know allure for me. When it comes to the heroine, I'm all for a feisty and confident character. But when faced with imminent danger or the fight for survival, I expect a certain level of submissiveness. I'm sure this shows how absolutely screwed up I am, but it is what it is.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429372i/860061._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>Teaser 1</b>
</i><br><i>
  <b>Q stood below, looking up at me. Slowly, he inserted his middle finger into his mouth and sucked. His eyes flashed with so much darkness I would never see the night again and not think of him. His tongue licked his finger with intoxicating grace. <br>My lips parted as he mesmerized me. Somehow, focusing on him helped dispel my panic, reminded me that Q might be bad, but he definitely wasn’t the worst.<br>It was almost a relief when he reached for my hip to hold me steady, his fingers biting into flesh. Slowly he poked his finger through the fabric of the dress and found the dampness on my thigh. His eyes shot to mine. “You continue to surprise me. I didn’t need to lick my finger after all.” <br>My cheeks pinked as he feathered his touch up my leg and stroked my entrance. His finger slipped in my wetness and a groan rumbled in his chest. He pulled me closer and like a pendulum I went—his to move where he wanted. Pressing his face on my chest, he thrust his finger inside me making my knees buckle and I swung slightly in my bindings. <br>His hand left my hip to wrap around my lower back, securing me tightly. “Ah, esclave. You continue to lie. Your body tells the truth.</b>
</i><br><br><i>
  <b>Teaser 2</b>
</i><br><i>
  <b>He reared back, his hand raised to strike. I fought the urge to curl into a little ball, and stared right into his turbulent gaze. “Do it. Hit me. At least the pain will leave a physical mark that you’ll have to see every day.”<br>He opened his mouth, but then shut it again. His hand dropped, settling limp on the bed. Something raw blazed in his gaze before he clambered off me, pacing in my small cage. <br>“What is your name?” he growled, still pacing. His suit crinkled, perfection marred. <br>“What does Q stand for?”<br>“What is your name?”<br>“Let me go and I’ll tell you.”<br>We stalemated, glaring once again. Day by day I was becoming a champion at staring competitions. <br>This one, though, I lost. Q’s gaze set fire to my blood. Smouldering and licking with unwanted lust. Misplaced lust. Lust that drove me mad with confusion and hatred for myself. <br>I dropped my eyes and waited. Just like that, I was his again. <br>An eerie sense of calm filled me. Obedience was a balm against the hardship of fighting. Why fight when I could make my life so much easier by becoming a robot? Turn off my feelings and do as he asked. <br>Q stepped forward, putting himself right between my legs. His belt was eye level and the heat blazing from his body cindered all my other emotions to dust. <br>He was male. I was female. That was all there was to it. <br>My hands moved on their own accord, reaching for his waist. Blissful vacancy filled me. I floated on a cloud of indifference as I pulled the leather free from loops and undid the buckle.</b>
</i><br><br><i>ARC courtesy of author in exchange for an honest review</i></span>

    <a title="La-Lionne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11644154-la-lionne"><img alt="La-Lionne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1458815714p2/11644154.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/669019175?book_show_action=true">Jul 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="La-Lionne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="La-Lionne" href="/user/show/11644154-la-lionne">La-Lionne</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18399439-tears-of-tess">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=action-packed">action-packed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=badly-written">badly-written</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=skipped-a-lot">skipped-a-lot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=could-not-finish">could-not-finish</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=mafia-gangs">mafia-gangs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=reviews-say-yay-i-say-nay">reviews-say-yay-i-say-nay</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=bdsm">bdsm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=dumb-heroine">dumb-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=own">own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=alpha-male-wannabe">alpha-male-wannabe</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer669019175" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11624677440516309818">I can't... I just... My god, the heroine of this book...<br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1435490679ra/15352784.gif' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>To say that this book is predictable would be an understatement of the century. <br/>The first twenty or so present of the book are uses to introduce us to the heroine and her boyfriend. They have the most boring relationship on the planet. She loves him, thinks he's great and hopes that he will propose to her. At the same time, every time she says something good about him, she always adds that he can't satisfy her sexually. He is so great, so </span>
  <span id="freeText11624677440516309818" style="display:none">I can't... I just... My god, the heroine of this book...<br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1435490679ra/15352784.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To say that this book is predictable would be an understatement of the century. <br>The first twenty or so present of the book are uses to introduce us to the heroine and her boyfriend. They have the most boring relationship on the planet. She loves him, thinks he's great and hopes that he will propose to her. At the same time, every time she says something good about him, she always adds that he can't satisfy her sexually. He is so great, so amazing, she just wished he would tie her up, or spank her once in a blue moon. But he is so great. Sometimes she even blabs it out loud, but he is all "don't be weird, let's forget you ever said that"<br>The boyfriend has planned a secret trip. The secret doesn't last long though. They get to the airport and are asked to show they traveling documents. Excitement dies when the girl at the airport asks "Do you want your bags checked all the way through Cancun?" Beside it being a badly planned secret, another thing bugged me; if they are traveling to Mexico, why would they want their bags checked somewhere else? What a stupid question to ask. <br>At some point the boyfriend whips it out a jewelry box and says "I got something for you". She is all "Aww." It turns out it's a promise bracelet. See, he is great! She just wishes he would bend her over over some furniture once in a while. But other than that, he is a fantastic boyfriend. Aw, and the bracelet is beautiful, it promises so much. Anywho. <br><br>They arrived to Cancun. She is all "I'll show you how much I love you," changes into a sexy little number and whips out a vibrator. Here I thought "Ok, it's happening, sexy time" <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1435492648ra/15352950.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I was sure her boyfriend was going to be all:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1435492803ra/15352954.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Nope!<br>We don't get to know what his reaction is, because she jumps in and starts explaining that she wanted to spice things up, starts apologizing and next thing you know, 20 seconds later he is coming while she is just lying there. But still, he is great, so great, she loves him so. <br>They go on to have a great time, cruising around on a scooter around Cancun. They stop to get a drink at some god forsaken place and she gets kidnapped by a group of dudes, who beet her boyfriend up and delivers her to Q. <br>Of course it's horrible, she just got kidnapped and sold to some dude in France. She still thinks of her boyfriend and how much she misses him. But damn if Q's sadistic ways doesn't make her feel good. But of course she get all hot and bothered for him, remember, one third of the book was used to tell to the readers about her fantasizing about kink. I can't help but think that her earlier fantasies were used to justify what happens later in the book. It's like saying "Yeah, it's horrible, but remember her wanting that in the beginning of the book? So it's all good."<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389064816ra/7981465.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>At some point later she gets an opportunity to escape and runs. She knows she is in France, but has not clue what part of the country. But she plans to get ahold of a phone and tell her boyfriend that she is on a way to the Australian embassy to get papers fixed and will be coming home. Son of a mother f*cker, you have no freaking clue where you are!!! Ugh!<br>She gets to barrow a phone with an intention to call her boyfriend to tell him where she is and who took her. It rings and rings, he doesn't pic up and she leaves him a voicemail while wondering "Omg, is he dead? Did they kill him, omg." At this pint she has been in captivity for three weeks.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393034766ra/8651635.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Dead people don't charge their phones, you dumb ass! <br>Don't even get me started on the fact that she cut her tracking device off, so she won't be fallowed, just to throw it on a floor of a moving car SHE WAS IN! The amount of stupidity this heroine possesses is mind-blowing. <br>Then there was some rape drama. Of course Q came running to rescue her. Remember how she got rid of her tracking device?<br>Then it turned out that he is not a bad guy. He actually buys women to save them. The fact that he threatened her not to escape, put a tracking device on her, used starvations as a punishment, allowed his friend to rape her with a knife handle and called her a bitch after she was raped by coupe of guys while trying to escape, is beyond the point. He is a good guy at heart, that's all author wants you to know. <br>Oh, and right after (the very same day he brought her back home after her attempted escape), she felt broken. Broken as in "He is my master, I belong to him, I will never run again. Do what you want with me."<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1435496030ra/15353193.gif" width="400" height="190" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I just had to DNF the book after that. I felt my brain cells were dying with every page I read. </span>
  <a data-text-id="11624677440516309818" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_669149436" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/669149436" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/669149436?book_show_action=true">Jul 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=2013-release">2013-release</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=emotional-rollercoaster">emotional-rollercoaster</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=arc-or-netgalley">arc-or-netgalley</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer669149436" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10936839605793173414"><br/>♦ <b>4 STARS. ♦</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429398i/860154._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429398i/860155._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Tears of Tess</b> is an emotional, intriguing and captivating story that starts out with a very ominous prologue that managed to grab my attention form the very first page. After that there are some more disturbing scenes, it <i>is</i> a kidnapping story after all, but nothing that went over the edge of being too dark or disturbing. <br/><br/><i>Tears of Tess</i> is the story of a young girl named <i>Tess Snow</i> who gets kidnapped while on vacation in Mexico. After that she is sold to a man who plans to own her as a</span>
  <span id="freeText10936839605793173414" style="display:none"><br>♦ <b>4 STARS. ♦</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429398i/860154._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429398i/860155._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Tears of Tess</b> is an emotional, intriguing and captivating story that starts out with a very ominous prologue that managed to grab my attention form the very first page. After that there are some more disturbing scenes, it <i>is</i> a kidnapping story after all, but nothing that went over the edge of being too dark or disturbing. <br><br><i>Tears of Tess</i> is the story of a young girl named <i>Tess Snow</i> who gets kidnapped while on vacation in Mexico. After that she is sold to a man who plans to own her as a slave...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"Three little words. <br>If anyone asked me what terrified me, stole my breath and made my life flicker before my eyes, I would say three little words. <br>I was sold."</b>
</blockquote><br><br>During a vacation in Cancun with her boyfriend Brax, Tess falls into the hands of a Mexican human trafficking orginazation. The men treat her like an object rather than a human being. She tries to fight them, but the more she struggles the worse her future might turn out to be.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"If you behave, you will be sold to a gentleman who will treat you like a prized possesion. Lavish attention on you. Buy you whatever you want."</b>
</blockquote><br><br>And then she's flown over to France and sold into the hands of her new Master, <b>Q Mercer</b>. A man whose commanding presense alone manages to make her tremble with fear and arouse her at the same time.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429398i/860156._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As the days pass by, Tess starts to form a friendship with some of the housemembers while at the same time learning more about her new Master. She's drawn to him, yet he manages to scare her away as well. He's a walking contradiction. One minute he seems concerned for her well-being, the next he's determined on breaking her and pushing her to see how far he can go before she cracks. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"You don't know anything, esclave. I want this. I've wanted this for too damn long, and you're wrong that it hurts. I'm not afraid of hurting you. I'm afraid of how far I'm willing to go."</b>
</blockquote><br><br>It's obvious Q has some demons in his past that still haunt him to this day. He seems tortured by his memories and his secret desires and Tess's presense seems to bring out the worst in him. Or is it the best? Both Tess and Q struggle with their inner conflicting emotions and desires. But together they seem to be able to help each other discover their true selves.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429398i/860157.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I would have thought that Q <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[had actually bought Tess and that he had a habbit of buying slaven and breaking them for his pleasure. But the reality was far from it. He turned out to be a savior rather than a monster. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> And maybe that's where the blurb can be a little misleading. It makes you think <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Q is this dark, disturbing monster with cruel tendencies, but in reality he does everything in his power to keep those dark thoughts at bay <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br>There were some contradictions theoughout the story that made the story a little less convincing at times, most of them involved <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Tess's emotions. They constantly went from one extreme to another which made it a little hard for me to truly be convinced by the reality of them. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br>The epilogue was told from Q's point of view which provided an interesting change of set-up and I really liked getting to know what was going through his head during those last few scenes. It made Q seem like an even more intriguing and fascinating character and I was glad the author decided to include those scenes from his POV. I was impressed with the way the author managed to revoke so many emotions with her lyrical writing style. She managed to make both Q and Tess fascinating characters and it was interesting to follow their journey throughout the story. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"Monsters find each other in the dark."</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429398i/860158.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Overall, <b>Tears of Tess</b> turned out to be a captivating story about loss, despair, love, hope, redemption and so much more. Pepper Winters managed to write a unique and memorable debut novel and I'm already looking forward to reading more of her work in the future! The story wasn't as dark and disturbing as I expected it to be, but I think that might be a good thing, because that way it might appeal to a wider range of readers! <br><br>So, don't let the blurb scare you off and find out for yourself just how far Q is really willing to go to show Tess his true nature...<br><br><br><b>~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429398i/860159.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>**ARC kindly provided by the author in exchange for an honest review**</i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="10936839605793173414" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1290057252" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1290057252" />
    <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously"><img alt="Rachel Reads Ravenously" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1539149211p2/14514998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1290057252?book_show_action=true">May 26, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel Reads Ravenously" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously">Rachel Reads Ravenously</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18399439-tears-of-tess">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Rachel Reads Ravenously by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine">Jasmine</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=new-adult-mania">new-adult-mania</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=i-wouldnt-tell-my-mama-i-read-this">i-wouldnt-tell-my-mama-i-read-this</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1290057252" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13809923138439056673"><b> 4 esclave stars! </b><br/><br/><b> <i> "Monsters find each other in the dark." </i> </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/tears%20of%20tess.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432634584i/14991869.png' alt=' photo tears of tess.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This is one of those books where I am kicking myself for not having read it already. To be fair, it's a dark one and I was afraid of it going in. But surprisingly, I expected it to be a lot darker than it was so I was very happy that I could read this book without freaking out (at least, as much as I expected to).<br/><br/><b> Tears of Tess </b> is about Tess, who goes on a surprise trip to Cancun, Mexico from Australia with her boyfriend Brax. The</span>
  <span id="freeText13809923138439056673" style="display:none"><b> 4 esclave stars! </b><br><br><b> <i> "Monsters find each other in the dark." </i> </b><br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/tears%20of%20tess.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432634584i/14991869.png" alt=" photo tears of tess.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This is one of those books where I am kicking myself for not having read it already. To be fair, it's a dark one and I was afraid of it going in. But surprisingly, I expected it to be a lot darker than it was so I was very happy that I could read this book without freaking out (at least, as much as I expected to).<br><br><b> Tears of Tess </b> is about Tess, who goes on a surprise trip to Cancun, Mexico from Australia with her boyfriend Brax. The two of them have been together for two years and while she loves him, Tess is a little underwhelmed in the bedroom department. She wants more excitement, more passion, more than just flat on her back. Having trouble communicating this, the couple just sort of avoids the elephant in the room. It's while they are out being tourists that Tess is taken, kidnapped and sold into the sex trade.<br><br>Tess finds herself as the new property of Q, a terrifying yet handsome Frenchman. Yet as much as Tess hates Q for who he is and what he represents, he is the only man who has ever been able to give her what she yearns for, and it brings her an immense amount of shame. As time goes by Tess is bewildered by his behavior and struggles with guilt over her feelings for Q and her devotion to Brax.<br><br><b> <i> “I hadn’t gone Stockholmy- I hated him, knew what he did was wrong, but my body, shit, my body didn’t care.” </i> </b><br><br>This is one of the few dark novels where I have genuinely ended up liking the antihero. He wasn't perfect, but he never cast blame on Tess for the situation she was in. In other dark novels, the guy always finds a way to wriggle himself out of the blame, and Q never did this. Q admitted what he was, a monster, but he took care of Tess in any way he was able to. Was her experience in his home all sunshine and rainbows? No, but it could have been much, much worse.<br><br>Ms. Winters is a great author because she threw the reader a curve ball and made them rethink everything they had previously read, and look at the facts in a new light. I literally read this book in one sitting because I was so riveted by the story I was reading. It's always so darn amazing to find a book like this, that captures your attention and doesn't let go until it's over.<br><br><b> <i> “Only think of me and what I’m doing. There is intimacy in pain esclave. Let me make your pain my pleasure.” </i> </b><br><br>So why not a perfect 5 stars? --&gt; <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I really took issue with the knife rape scene with the Russian and how Q had let him get that far. I was feeling the same way Tess was after when she realized as her master he was supposed to protect her and he didn't, he turned away. I also took issue with the rape scene, I felt it was a blatant "see, it COULD be worse!" addition to the story to make Q look better when it wasn't needed. It wasn't needed because we found out later he was rescuing all of these girls, so he was in fact already a good guy.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>So now that it's 3 AM my time, I'm going to make myself go to sleep and not start the second book. At least I'll try.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="13809923138439056673" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1234251452" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1234251452" />
    <a title="Jessica&#39;s Totally Over The Top Book Obsession" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/28967089-jessica-s-totally-over-the-top-book-obsession"><img alt="Jessica&#39;s Totally Over The Top Book Obsession" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1511556834p2/28967089.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1234251452?book_show_action=true">Mar 22, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica&#39;s Totally Over The Top Book Obsession" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica&#39;s Totally Over The Top Book Obsession" href="/user/show/28967089-jessica-s-totally-over-the-top-book-obsession">Jessica&#39;s Totally Over The Top Book Obsession</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28967089-jessica-s-totally-over-the-top-book-obsession?shelf=meh-reads">meh-reads</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1234251452" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9211766100141885606">2.5 stars<br/><br/><br/>I really, really wanted to like this book. I read the reviews, and thought it would blow my mind. Something different. The story plot sounded great, and the reviews for the most part are great, but I just couldn't connect to this book. It wasn't even as dark as I expected. I have read a handful of Dark romances, and loved them, but this one didn't do much for me. I didn't really get it. Tess gave me whiplash she was so all over the place. I didn't connect to her at all. She made no sens</span>
  <span id="freeText9211766100141885606" style="display:none">2.5 stars<br /><br /><br />I really, really wanted to like this book. I read the reviews, and thought it would blow my mind. Something different. The story plot sounded great, and the reviews for the most part are great, but I just couldn't connect to this book. It wasn't even as dark as I expected. I have read a handful of Dark romances, and loved them, but this one didn't do much for me. I didn't really get it. Tess gave me whiplash she was so all over the place. I didn't connect to her at all. She made no sense to me. Q did nothing for me. Q was a very one dimensional character for me. I felt no depth, and nothing drew me to him. I didn't get what Tess saw in him. He just fell flat. I found myself bored for a good part of this book. The sex in this book did NOTHING for me, and their relationship made no sense to me. It took me 3 days to finish this book, and I normally whip through a book in a day. I can't even bring myself to read the next book in this series. I'm just like Whatevz! </span>

Berg</i><br>2. Dominic by L.A. Casey<br>3. The Boy Who Sneaks in My Bedroom Window by Kirsty Moseley<br>4. When the Sun Goes Down by Erin Noelle<br>5. Freefall by Tess Oliver<br>6. All for You by Kate Perry<br>7. Until Trevor by Aurora Rose Reynolds<br>8. Searching For Moore by Julie A. Richman<br>9. In a Heartbeat by Hilary Storm<br>10. Tears of Tess by Pepper Winters<br><br>To read a blurb about each book -&gt; <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://bit.ly/1tWvS9E">http://bit.ly/1tWvS9E</a><br>*******************************************<br><br>A <b>dark romance</b> that has all the ingredients for a great book: <br><b>*</b>Kidnapping<br><b>*</b>Slavery<br><b>*</b>Sandy Beaches<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/487375.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>*3.5 Q stars*</b><br><br>A year ago this book was recommended to me and when I saw it on Netgalley, the other day, I thought it was time to finally read it. <br><br>One reason I enjoy dark books is because they evoke all kinds of emotions from the reader. Yes, I'm an<b> emotional junkie</b> when it comes to books. I love the thrill of being shocked and at times having to cover my eyes when something either scares me or disgust me. <b>
  <blockquote>"...fantasy turned into realities..."</blockquote>
</b><b>Tess</b> fantasizes about having a darker sex life than she currently has with her boyfriend. She wants its rough and to be owned while her boyfriend likes their simple relationship. <br><br><b>Tess's fantasies become a realty when she is kidnapped on a trip to Mexico and given to a man, <b>Q</b>, as a bribe. </b> <br><br>Tess's inner dialogue was frustrating for me. Being that she was wishy-washy at times caused me to not connect with her character. When she started blaming herself for being kidnapped because she always wished for a rougher sex like that just didn't feel genuine. While I may not have been rooting for Tess...I was intrigued by the man she called Q. My driving force to finish the book was <b>Q</b> because I wanted to know more about his mysterious past. Plus I enjoyed that he was a control freak who was remote and aloof. <br><br><b>TEARS OF TESS</b> is Ms. Winters debut novel. I can see why lots of friends love this book. I've been told that book 2 is the favorite among most who've read the series. I'll be curious to see where the story takes Q and Tess. Just because my stars weren't 4 or 5 doesn't mean I won't continue on with the series. Some of my favorite series I have 3 starred the first book; "The Addicted Series" and one of my favorite books last year was "Dirty Red" (book 2) even though I gave the first book 3 stars. <br><br><b>SERIES:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18134894.Tears_of_Tess__Monsters_in_the_Dark___1_" title="Tears of Tess (Monsters in the Dark, #1) by Pepper Winters" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1378381640s/18398089.jpg" alt="Quintessentially Q (Monsters in the Dark, #2) by Pepper Winters" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/19015729.Twisted_Together__Monsters_in_the_Dark___3_" title="Twisted Together (Monsters in the Dark, #3) by Pepper Winters" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1387550441s/19015729.jpg" alt="Twisted Together (Monsters in the Dark, #3) by Pepper Winters" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_670336914" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/670336914" />
    <a title="Rosalinda *KRASNORADA*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12788865-rosalinda-krasnorada"><img alt="Rosalinda *KRASNORADA*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583582487p2/12788865.jpg" /></a>

<span id="freeTextContainer17618716837058262415"><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429566i/860676._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Let’s keep this short and sweet. I am not rating the book because I don’t think that’s fair right now. I enjoyed certain parts of Tess’s story but I didn’t enjoy another parts and rolled my eyes to no end.<br/>Tess is a girl who has dark desires but she has a vanilla lovely boyfriend. Brax takes her to Mexico for a romantic trip but life has different plans for Tess. She’s suddenly kidnapped and sold to Q, a French hot Master who is (apparently) a dark monster.<br/><br/>I want to remark ‘apparently’ because he</span>
  <span id="freeText17618716837058262415" style="display:none"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429566i/860676._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Let’s keep this short and sweet. I couldn’t connect with him because he was a dark monster sometimes but one minute later he was sweet and nice. And Tess? Don’t let me start with her better. <br><br>I think the story was well written and the sex scenes were scorching hot and all but I have a problem, I need a coherent plot to get into a story. I think Pepper will be able to write better stories in the future, this one unfortunately was not for me.<br><br>I won’t say anything else about the story because I don’t want to spoil it for you.<br><br>I also want to mention this might be a case of it’s me and not you book so pls check out those wonderful 5 stars reviews.     <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
