        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer671501951" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3328666604470793816"><b>3 Not-at-all-what-I-was-expecting Stars<br/><br/><i>A human is adaptable. A human heart is not.</i></b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429736i/861070._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='180' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Human minds and souls are unique and complex. Powerful and capable of both cruelty and tenderness. No one is to blame for their personal choices. Nobody should be ashamed of their preferences. Fantasies are to be played out. Monsters become dangerous when caged for too long and birds should be let free to fly.<br/><br/><b>Tess Snow</b> is a young woman feeling alone and undesirable. Unfilled passions and fantasies overwhelm her day</span>
  <span id="freeText3328666604470793816" style="display:none"><b>3 Not-at-all-what-I-was-expecting Stars<br><br><i>A human is adaptable. A human heart is not.</i></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429736i/861070._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Human minds and souls are unique and complex. Powerful and capable of both cruelty and tenderness. No one is to blame for their personal choices. Nobody should be ashamed of their preferences. Fantasies are to be played out. Monsters become dangerous when caged for too long and birds should be let free to fly.<br><br><b>Tess Snow</b> is a young woman feeling alone and undesirable. Unfilled passions and fantasies overwhelm her day and dreams, feelings that her boyfriend doesn't comprehend or is willing to fulfill. Unspeakable things and dark desires confuse and leave her craving more.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429736i/861071.png" width="400" height="143" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A trip to Mexico should be a rehearsal honeymoon, but it turns into her worst nightmare when she is kidnapped and sold to human traffickers. Another lost soul, a woman bartered like an animal.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“My life was complete. Happy, content, everything neat and perfect.<br>Then it all changed.<br>I was sold.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429736i/861072._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Brutalized and scared, she refuses to bow down and break. She will fight her captors and she won't submit. Even if her Master, awakens all her deepest and darkest passions.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429372i/860061._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="800" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Q. Mercer</b> is a man of many faces. A ruthless businessman, a cruel master, a tender companion. Tormented by personal demons, craving twisted and dark fantasies, scared of himself and of feelings, he is an enigma that he can't deny one thing. He wants Tess, his perfect, unbroken <i>Esclave</i> and he will do anything to possess her completely. Kill, let the beast free, even set her free...<br><br><i>
  <b>I want to hurt you. I want to own you. I want to devour you. I want to make you mine.</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429736i/861073._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>That's our exciting and very well written story. Now let's see what issues I had with it...<br><br>Me at the beginning:<br><b>Here's to a dominant, sexually frustrating, dark and twisted read!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429736ra/861074.gif" width="400" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Me now:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429736ra/861075.gif" width="400" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There... I admit it. I made a rookie mistake. I tried to comprehend and fell in love with a story just by a blurb and a few teasers. I let my enthusiasm carry me away and I got in mind that I knew this story was about. I was expecting a twisted story of forbidden passions and when I didn't get it, I was disappointed. So the first to blame is myself. <br><br>Then there are the characters, that managed to confuse and well, bore me a little. This story isn't about seasoned, self assured dominants and submissives. It's about people mainly ashamed and afraid of their desires, constantly doubting themselves and their actions. Second-guessing one other, running away and always craving assurance. <br><br>This a great story and a well written debut novel by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7151973.Pepper_Winters" title="Pepper Winters" rel="nofollow noopener">Pepper Winters</a>. I recommend it to readers that want a dramatic story about a darker aspect of love. The reality of slaves and women broken beyond repair. About the desires we can't admit to ourselves in the light of day. Do not expect mindfuckery. This a story about forgiveness and redemption and finding the one that completes your soul.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429736i/861076.png" width="400" height="217" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Overall, a good, solid read, that left me craving more. No matter, I will keep my eye out for any next books by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7151973.Pepper_Winters" title="Pepper Winters" rel="nofollow noopener">Pepper Winters</a>! ;)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/614910.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Pre-release review</i><br><i><b>*TEASER*</b><br><br> He reared back, his hand raised to strike. I fought the urge to curl into a little ball, and stared right into his turbulent gaze. “Do it. Hit me. At least the pain will leave a physical mark that you’ll have to see every day.”<br>He opened his mouth, but then shut it again. His hand dropped, settling limp on the bed. Something raw blazed in his gaze before he clambered off me, pacing in my small cage.<br>“What is your name?” he growled, still pacing. His suit crinkled, perfection marred.<br>“What does Q stand for?”<br>“What is your name?”<br>“Let me go and I’ll tell you.”<br>We stalemated, glaring once again. Day by day I was becoming a champion at staring competitions.<br>This one, though, I lost. Q’s gaze set fire to my blood. Smouldering and licking with unwanted lust. Misplaced lust. Lust that drove me mad with confusion and hatred for myself.<br>I dropped my eyes and waited. Just like that, I was his again.<br>An eerie sense of calm filled me. Obedience was a balm against the hardship of fighting. Why fight when I could make my life so much easier by becoming a robot? Turn off my feelings and do as he asked.<br>Q stepped forward, putting himself right between my legs. His belt was eye level and the heat blazing from his body cindered all my other emotions to dust.<br>He was male. I was female. That was all there was to it.<br>My hands moved on their own accord, reaching for his waist. Blissful vacancy filled me. I floated on a cloud of indifference as I pulled the leather free from loops and undid the buckle.</i> <br><br><b>In the name of everything that is dark and twisted, what new gem do we have here????</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/590356.gif" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The teasers keep coming...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429373i/860062.jpg" width="240" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429373i/860063._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="550" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I CAN'T FREAKING WAIT!!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429736ra/861077.gif" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>For whatever happens, for all the heartbreak and mindf*ckery that awaits I blame Soraya, her promotion, her recommendation, HELL even her pics... You wonderful crazy-ass babe...</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/481549.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>*ARC courtesy of the author, the wonderful <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7151973.Pepper_Winters" title="Pepper Winters" rel="nofollow noopener">Pepper Winters</a>, in exchange for an honest review*</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380222758i/536227.gif" width="400" height="252" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>08/17:<br><b>Just got my copy!!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429736ra/861078.gif" width="400" height="320" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="3328666604470793816" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer3776167119666068838"><b>
  <u> 2,5 confusing and not too dark stars</u>
</b><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429785ra/861226.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I have no words!I expected this book to be awesome,amazing,a mindfuck.Oh wait... it was a mindfuck... in a bad way...It was one of those book that you read and wonder <i>"What was the puprose of this book?"</i>First of all,let's say that it was not as dark as it's been promoted to be.Aside from the cruel start and a few other moments the book was lightly dark or sometimes not dark at all.<br/><br/><br/><b>
  <u>Plot:</u>
</b><br/>Her name is Tess and she has an ostensibly good life.She seems hap</span>
  <span id="freeText3776167119666068838" style="display:none"><b>
  <u> 2,5 confusing and not too dark stars</u>
</b><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429785ra/861226.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have no words!I expected this book to be awesome,amazing,a mindfuck.Oh wait... it was a mindfuck... in a bad way...It was one of those book that you read and wonder <i>"What was the puprose of this book?"</i>First of all,let's say that it was not as dark as it's been promoted to be.Aside from the cruel start and a few other moments the book was lightly dark or sometimes not dark at all.<br><br><br><b>
  <u>Plot:</u>
</b><br>Her name is Tess and she has an ostensibly good life.She seems happy as long as she ignores her parents.Her boyfriend is so sweet,caring that you will feel jealous towards her.Yet,that is not enough for her.Her body shimmers for sinful things but her boyfriend is the vanilla guy who cant fullfill her fantasies.<br><br>A casual trip to Mexico doesnt end up as it was expected to.They kidnapp her.<b>They steal her freedom.</b>However our MC is strong and doesnt even think that giving up is an option.<br><br><b>" I would never give up. I would fight until I died; I’d teach the kidnappers they stole the wrong girl if they wanted meek and broken."</b><br><br>I loved her so far.Her determination to live made me praise her.Never the less Tess's fate is sealed.She is the bribe of a Rushian guy to Q.<br><br>Enter Q,<br>He is a French guy who <b>NEEDS TO ATTEND FRENCH LESSONS</b>.Q is supposed to be a sadistic master?!Errmm I'm not sure if he was sadistic or deranged.The one moment he was all bossy and domineering , the next one he was talkative and a normal billionaire.I couldnt connect with Q.His character confused me a lot.I'm still not sure if he was a good person or not.<br><br><br><b>Biggests turn offs:</b><br>The French,oh boy the French....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429785ra/861227.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>LOL it's not that I'm an expert in French but it was TOO obvious that the author didnt speak a word at French.The verbs in French are NOT the same at every person like in English,they change.For those who dont speak the language it wont be a problem but heck when I was reading French part I was doing a mental editing or I was LoLing, <s>sorry</s>.<br>The encouraging thing is that the author has taken action and is solving this probem so hopefully if you read the actual and final book those parts will be edited.<br><br>HUGE SPOILER AND WTF MOMENTS!<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[She gets raped and then she spends the night with Q?I understand that the author wanted to make it up for her but it was such an urealistic moment.Usually the rape victims dont tend to have sex a few hours after their abuse.The most annoying though was that after that she becomes attached to him just because he did that to her and she's curious about his past *facepalm*And WTH was the whole Q's mental speech that he wanted to rape her?HUH?? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Overall I didnt like it.It had a kickass start and definitely potential.The author's writing is amazing and I will read her future books but this one simply didnt work for me.Not being able to connect with the characters is one of the most awful things that can happen to a reader.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380349178ra/703259.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><i>Buddy read with Pavlina &lt;3</i><br><br><b>Arc kindly provided by the author in exchange for an honest review!</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1361616269" />
    <a title="CC" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12625026-cc"><img alt="CC" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1558473771p2/12625026.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1361616269?book_show_action=true">Aug 11, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="CC" class="user" itemprop="url" name="CC" href="/user/show/12625026-cc">CC</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

      <a href="/user/show/27276528-liz">✰ Liz ✰ </a>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12625026-cc?shelf=dirty-f-in-talkers">dirty-f-in-talkers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12625026-cc?shelf=darkish-to-depths-of-hell">darkish-to-depths-of-hell</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12625026-cc?shelf=mistress-ccs-dungeon">mistress-ccs-dungeon</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12625026-cc?shelf=action">action</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1361616269" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9873183746591497030"><b>4.5 “Tu es à moi” Stars</b><br/><br/>The story of Tess and Q is a complicated one layered with an array of emotions due to the nature of their introduction. From the beginning, Tess is confronted with a multitude of physical and emotional assaults, but she is adamant about not losing her true self. What she does find is a man that can give her what has been missing from her life…pain, pleasure and unadulterated dominance. However, what is the price Tess must pay to submit to her desires?<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445580713i/16677009._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Tess is a strong chara</span>
  <span id="freeText9873183746591497030" style="display:none"><b>4.5 “Tu es à moi” Stars</b><br><br>The story of Tess and Q is a complicated one layered with an array of emotions due to the nature of their introduction. From the beginning, Tess is confronted with a multitude of physical and emotional assaults, but she is adamant about not losing her true self. What she does find is a man that can give her what has been missing from her life…pain, pleasure and unadulterated dominance. However, what is the price Tess must pay to submit to her desires?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445580713i/16677009._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Tess is a strong character. I liked her from the beginning. While facing adversity and the unthinkable, she toughened up and fought to protect the only thing she could claim for herself. Her transition throughout this book made me question her motivations (and sanity) at times but Tess’ persevered and I had to admire her for that.<br><br><b> “I needed a safety mechanism, something to protect my soul like a suit of armour in battle.”</b><br><br>Q is definitely an acquired taste. He is a broken soul who believes he cannot be healed until he meets Tess. With Tess’ inner strength and ability to freely submit to Q, he begins to trust and wants to unleash his most sadistic desires without being deemed a monster. By the end of the book, my opinion of Q considerably changed. Did he completely win me over? I would say, “Hell yes!” lol.<br><br><b> “He whispered, “I’m not afraid of hurting you. I’m afraid of how far I’m willing to go.”</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445580818i/16677029._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is my first Pepper Winters book and I thoroughly enjoyed her writing style, as she has a way of drawing in the reader to each scene. I especially like how she described each character by addressing not only their physicality but also their scent, touch, taste and subtle movements or nuances that make a character unique. She also aptly captured the emotion and mood of each scene and I felt the physical tension whether sexual or torturous. After meeting Tess and Q, I cannot get their story from my mind. I will be moving forward learn more about the journey of Esclave and the Maître.<br><br><br><br><i>Note: Thanks to the Shhluts for a fabulous Buddy Read in preparation for the Shh...LIVE Chat with Pepper Winters on October 24 at 6 pm EST!!<br> <br>Special thanks to the ladies who recommended this book to me: Liz, Loyda, Hawkey, Snow and Huyla!! <br></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="9873183746591497030" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/932942819?book_show_action=true">May 09, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer932942819" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12160621422205282414"><b><u>Reread:6/12/17</u><br/><br/><br/>5 <i>'Captivating'</i> Stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zps6e4e810b.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420952144i/13296905._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo image_zps6e4e810b.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Brax surprised Tess to a vacation to Mexico. Tess thought that this was her chance to relax, spend time with her loving boyfriend, and to figure out who was she.<br/><br/><b>“This trip would allow me to inspect who I truly was, to be honest, and find the real me."</b><br/><br/>Tress loves her boyfriend Brax. He's everything you could ever want in a guy. He was loving, supportive,sweet, kind, and <i>safe</i>. They both loved each other and there's nothing they wouldn't do for each other. But</span>
  <span id="freeText12160621422205282414" style="display:none"><b><u>Reread:6/12/17</u><br><br><br>5 <i>'Captivating'</i> Stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zps6e4e810b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420952144i/13296905._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps6e4e810b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Brax surprised Tess to a vacation to Mexico. Tess thought that this was her chance to relax, spend time with her loving boyfriend, and to figure out who was she.<br><br><b>“This trip would allow me to inspect who I truly was, to be honest, and find the real me."</b><br><br>Tress loves her boyfriend Brax. He's everything you could ever want in a guy. He was loving, supportive,sweet, kind, and <i>safe</i>. They both loved each other and there's nothing they wouldn't do for each other. But there's a problem. Tess wants <i>more</i>. She doesn't want sweet love-making, she wants domination, hard fucking, pain, and submission. <br><br><b>I needed Brax to be rough because I needed to be claimed.</b><br><br>She doesn't have that with Brax, and she wonders <i>what's wrong with me?</i><br><br>While they were sight-seeing on a scooter, they got thirsty so they stopped for drinks. Tress immediately had this bad feeling. She was anxious and had this feeling in her stomach. First she was with her lovely Brax and then seconds later she was <b>kidnapped.</b><br><br><a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zps5bf51612.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420952144i/13296906._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps5bf51612.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>She was scared and beaten. She didn't know where she was or who took her. What did they want from her. The next thing she know was that <b>she.was.sold</b>. No matter what she went through or happens, she would fight. She would find freedom again, and she would not break.<br><br><b>I couldn’t be sucked into depression and give up. I would <i>never</i> give up. I would fight until I died.</b><br><br>She finally arrives to her new home. The home that she was sold into the owner of the house, the monster who bought her. She meets her new master Q.Mercer, and she became <i>enclave</i>.<br><br><b>His gaze unclothed and terrified me. Everything about him screamed ruthlessness and power. He held himself proud and regal as if this was his castle and I was the latest subject.</b><br><br>That's when shit started going down. <br><br>I really enjoyed this book. I haven't read any dark, kidnap, mysteries books in along time and I'm glad I read this. Through this whole thing I was..shhhh(secret)..<i>wet</i>. Q...[moans] is delish. That man is rich, sexy, alpha, french, and sexy. He was the complete package. <br><br><a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zps00c1b3a6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420952144i/13296907._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps00c1b3a6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Is there light beneath darkness?<br><br>Q is also broken that's why they connected so good. I loved how their relationship developed really well. This is off topic but at the beginning I kinda thought that Brax is..gay. I mean the guy is like a total nun..sorry Tess. Anyways..have two dark and twisted monsters found each other?<br><br><a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zps12ee2885.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420952144i/13296908._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps12ee2885.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Amazing and dark book. I really loved it and can't wait to start the second one. This is my first book by this author and I can assure you I will be reading more of her work. It's a really nice feeling when you read a book written by someone I unknown and you love it. It makes you proud. Anyways..overall amazing book.<br><br><a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zps8d22ec59.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420952144i/13296909._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps8d22ec59.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“I did the unthinkable: I broke myself, and fell for my master.</b></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer697000356" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer7717369369001665683"><b>5 Delicious, engaging and gripping stars*****</b><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/30A194BB-1556-4E9A-8487-471A151EC6E5_zpsylfgxdrs.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1401830078i/9854975._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 30A194BB-1556-4E9A-8487-471A151EC6E5_zpsylfgxdrs.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>Eeek I fell in love with this book, I fell in love with this journey but above all I fell hook line and sinker with these Characters, Q and Tess's story is passionate and yet beautiful at the same time. <br/><br/><br/>To me this was a story about finding the depths of our inner selves or mainly Tess's inner self and how both Tess and Q found and are still finding themselves, am I making any sense? <br/><br/><br/><b>Let me explain</b><br/><br/>Tess was made into a family that didn't want her, n</span>
  <span id="freeText7717369369001665683" style="display:none"><b>5 Delicious, engaging and gripping stars*****</b><br><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/30A194BB-1556-4E9A-8487-471A151EC6E5_zpsylfgxdrs.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1401830078i/9854975._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 30A194BB-1556-4E9A-8487-471A151EC6E5_zpsylfgxdrs.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Eeek I fell in love with this book, I fell in love with this journey but above all I fell hook line and sinker with these Characters, Q and Tess's story is passionate and yet beautiful at the same time. <br><br><br>To me this was a story about finding the depths of our inner selves or mainly Tess's inner self and how both Tess and Q found and are still finding themselves, am I making any sense? <br><br><br><b>Let me explain</b><br><br>Tess was made into a family that didn't want her, nor loved her this to me is unfathomable but yes there were no feelings lost here, therefore she is feeling lost and not really feeling like she has a place in the world so ends up with lovable Brax, Tess is studying architecture at university and Brax works hard they have this small little world that they've built together all that equals to <b>CONTENT</b> but sometimes we don't want content do we? And because they're busy and Brax is a very much missionary, simple, naïve and a BORING male (I had a few issues with Brax to be honest but I digress) above all Tess is seeking more so they go on holiday its planned by Brax and Tess is wanting to rekindle there relationship and there's something inside her that NEEDS something extra, sexually something darker. So off they go to the unknown and to find themselves again. <br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/gifs/14251827-754F-4F36-BF02-4C8E4149233A_zps0g7cdl6o.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1401733698ra/9839912.gif" alt=" photo 14251827-754F-4F36-BF02-4C8E4149233A_zps0g7cdl6o.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Mexico is where they end up and that leaves them in a vulnerable position, Brax made me cross here I just found him to be selfish wanting what he wanted to do and here we now have Tess getting into the world of slavery, being kidnapped and barcoded as a number <b>She's been brought</b><br><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>Brax. My life. My happy, happy world dissolved and left me in hell.</blockquote>
</b><br><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"Accept that you are no longer whoever you were. You are to forget about your past 'cause you will never see it again."</blockquote>
</b> <br><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/gifs/butterflygif_zps1f490c89.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402050026ra/9887543.gif" alt=" photo butterflygif_zps1f490c89.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Therefore she's scared but she's fighting and she will escape. She's been brought by our dashing sexy, arousing and intruiging Master Q he's French and now Tess becomes Esclave, this is where things turn up a notch and where Tess feels hopeless 'maybe' but most definitely is struck in awe by Q she is turned on by him, and there's just some serious wowza chemistry going on. What can I say he's like a magnet she doesn't want to feel the way she does but she most definitely does, but he's dangerous and hell I have a feeling this is just the start to getting DARKER.<br><br><br> <a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/ACE0536A-7C30-400B-9C3F-70CEA5D95122_zpsnvrgsux0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402206285i/9907584._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo ACE0536A-7C30-400B-9C3F-70CEA5D95122_zpsnvrgsux0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Tess has always been seeking something extra, with her fantasies at night the way she wanted to be with Brax maybe it lies with her upbringing and feeling lonely. She is a strong cookie though if there was ever a heroine I enjoyed to read Tess would be it, She is Fierce and strong willed and most definitely a fighter. And that is what Q is likewise drawn to esclave' because Q has never had a Slave that he has wanted to keep, one that he wants to be equal to and this is just the start , I think things are about to turn sinister and on a level of Dark I'd say this is low key to be honest but there's that edge that kept me on the edge of my seat and kept me gripped to find out what's coming next. <br><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/08F506E6-36ED-4EE6-B7DC-5C7B9F3371E3_zpszomqxnys.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402206285i/9907582._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 08F506E6-36ED-4EE6-B7DC-5C7B9F3371E3_zpszomqxnys.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>so to sum up</b><br><br>This is a book about freedom in every sense of the word, seriously look deeper, there's something vulnerable and I absolutely found Pepper Winters writing to grab hold of my every feeling, I was cross, angry, annoyed, sad, upset, intrigued and gripped yes I've found a new favourite author to love. <br><br><br>Would I recommend it: <b>Yes</b><br><br>Would I re-read it? <b>eventually yes but I've got the rest of the series to read yet</b><br><br>Would I read anything else that this author writes? <b>Yes yes and yes.</b> <br><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/B1301812-0865-4E1C-BD6B-53D369FC61C5_zpssnvrlc00.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><br>Onto the next.... <br><br>And a big hugeee hug to my girl Daisy honestly you definitely need to team up with someone when reading this series as I found chatting to Daisy for me enabled me to express my feelings and hold my hand while or listen to my moans LOL girl your the best &lt;3<br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/gifs/hugginggif_zpsee1d1e49.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer693625334" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15059048470425346646">Review posted on <a href='http://waytoohotbooks.blogspot.com/2013/08/arc-review-tears-of-tess-by-pepper.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Way Too Hot Books</a><br/> <br/>I am sorry, but I just don't like it...<br/><br/><br/> I have to admit that I wasn't sure about writing review for this book. This will be short.<br/><br/> Tears of Tess first got my attention because of pretty cover. After reading book description, I was sold. Dark, hot, erotic - check. Taboo, twisted, Stockholmish - check. Yes, my inner perv wa</span>
  <span id="freeText15059048470425346646" style="display:none">Review posted on <a href="http://waytoohotbooks.blogspot.com/2013/08/arc-review-tears-of-tess-by-pepper.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Way Too Hot Books</a><br /> <br />I am sorry, but I just don't like it...<br /><br /><br /> I have to admit that I wasn't sure about writing review for this book. I always feel bad when I don't have lot of good things to say about ARC I requested. But then again it is honesty that is appreciated, right? This will be short.<br /><br /> Tears of Tess first got my attention because of pretty cover. After reading book description, I was sold. Dark, hot, erotic - check. Taboo, twisted, Stockholmish - check. Yes, my inner perv was having a blast. Then my co-blogger Tanja over at Ja čitam, a ti? told me that I probably could get advanced copy of this book. I was over the moon. Few days later and there it was in my inbox. That's where everything went downhill. Why? Well, that would be a little longer list.<br /><br />1. I love taboo themes. Stockholm syndrome is on the top of my perv-list. (I know - don't judge me.) You would think that Tears of Tess would be perfect for me. Wrong. I didn't find it believable at all.<br /><br />2. Badly labeled. I understand that new adult is big hit now, but this book is not new adult. At least not by my standards. Tears of Tess is taboo erotica no matter how old main heroin is. I know authors like to use all kind of tricks to get attention, but please, don't label your books as something they are not.<br /><br />3. Storyline. It started really interesting, but than it all... I don't know. Something happened and I just started to notice all cracks in the plot. It has interesting premise, but it's too much like faerie tales about princesses who have to save kingdom by marring monster-king who is actually good, but he just forgot all about it because of some curse.<br /><br />4. Tess and Q. So many times I just wanted to slap both of them or to finally stop reading.<br /><br /> One thing that I liked - steamy scenes were interesting.<br /><br /> Maybe it is just me. Maybe I read it at the wrong moment. Maybe you will love this book. Or I have finally outgrown this type of literature. I don't know. If you are intrigued by dark erotica, you should read Tears of Tess. If you read Dark Duet series by S.J. Roberts and you think that Q is new Caleb, lover your expectations.<br /><br />***Copy of the book provided by author in exchange for honest review***</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer659390191" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer846862766986238045"><a href='http://www.amazon.com/Tears-Tess-Monsters-Pepper-Winters-ebook/dp/B00EV9LSJI/' rel='nofollow noopener'>ON SALE or $.99!</a><br/><br/><i>Kidnapped. Drugged. Stolen.</i><br/><br/>SIGH. I LOVED THIS BOOK.<br/><br/>Pepper Winters has amazing story-telling skills.<br/><br/>The change Tess undergoes as a character from this... naive, slightly desperate girl to a very strong female character in the end was amazing to see. I STRUGGLED WITH TESS. In the beginning. So it should say something that by the end I was giving her a fictional high-five girl power kpow! With every blow she takes, she just comes out stronger and better, and trust me, she takes a lo</span>
  <span id="freeText846862766986238045" style="display:none"><a href="http://www.amazon.com/Tears-Tess-Monsters-Pepper-Winters-ebook/dp/B00EV9LSJI/" rel="nofollow noopener">ON SALE or $.99!</a><br /><br /><i>Kidnapped. Drugged. Stolen.</i><br /><br />SIGH. I LOVED THIS BOOK.<br /><br />Pepper Winters has amazing story-telling skills.<br /><br />The change Tess undergoes as a character from this... naive, slightly desperate girl to a very strong female character in the end was amazing to see. I STRUGGLED WITH TESS. In the beginning. So it should say something that by the end I was giving her a fictional high-five girl power kpow! With every blow she takes, she just comes out stronger and better, and trust me, she takes a lot of blows. It was awesome.<br /><br />Q is...<br />I can't tell you about Q, because the unraveling of his character was done so well I don't want to say ANYTHING about him, just so you get to experience him.<br />But I will tell you how his character made me feel.<br />SO.CONFLICTED.<br />One second he's human, next he turns into a monster. My mind was spinning and I FREAKING LOVED IT. I loved Q so much!<br />I loved that the author doesn't make excuses for him, it is what it is. Take it or leave it.<br /><br />If you're reading the book for the sweet love despite the odds just step away cause this is not it. The connection these two share is dark and twisted and sick but it works. It's co-dependency on a whole another level. They're good apart but together they're explosive. And it made sense and I understood it.<br /><br />If I had to, I'd say this book was 50SoG done right, but it feels like I'm downplaying it cause it's so much more.<br />Also, I'm not a shadey books fan.<br /><br />If you can handle the abuse and just how graphic it is, it's so worth it. I'm just gonna write out that this book comes with trigger warning for good reason. Yes, there's rape. Yes, it's brutal.<br /><br />I don't even have to say there are graphic sex scenes.<br /><br />OH! Totally forgot to mention the epilogue! FREAKING LOVED IT. LOVED LOVED LOVED.<br /><br />Overall, TESS DELIVERS. Pepper Winters totally delivers and I'm so glad I got to read this book cause I was bursting at the seams waiting for it. I'm really excited for uh... To see what else she comes up with. AMAYZIN.</span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1053602034" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6112273930878068998"><br/>My reaction when I see Dark Romance...<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1410975340ra/11178201.gif' width='480' height='220' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Yep, That me!! They scare me big time!! I can’t stand assault, violence, rape, Trafficking. These are usually elements for my nightmare. At some point I needed to be brave enough to come out of my comfort zone that’s when “Tears of Tess” came along.<br/><br/><b>Three little words.<br/>If anyone asked what I was most afraid of, what terrified me, stole my breath, and made my life flicker before my eyes, I would say three little words.<br/><br/><i>I was sold.</i></b> <br/><br/>Just first few lines from Prolo</span>
  <span id="freeText6112273930878068998" style="display:none"><br>My reaction when I see Dark Romance...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1410975340ra/11178201.gif" width="480" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yep, That me!! They scare me big time!! I can’t stand assault, violence, rape, Trafficking. These are usually elements for my nightmare. At some point I needed to be brave enough to come out of my comfort zone that’s when “Tears of Tess” came along.<br><br><b>Three little words.<br>If anyone asked what I was most afraid of, what terrified me, stole my breath, and made my life flicker before my eyes, I would say three little words.<br><br><i>I was sold.</i></b> <br><br>Just first few lines from Prologue and I dived into this story. Yes! I was terrified beyond belief but the story from Tess’s eyes made it real. She was a victim of human trafficking! I hoped and prayed that she stayed strong, she’d escape, she’d fight for her freedom and never breakdown but what followed after she was sold was worth reading.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410975340i/11178202._SX540_.jpg" width="670" height="310" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was so captivated by this story not a typical Stockholm syndrome cliché. Tess was definitely captive in Q’s mansion always plotting for her escape, never obeying her master. Series of events leads her to see different dimensions to Q. He was not a captor but a saviour, time and again he proves her that she is safe with him, he would always protect her. Q’s an enigma, he had an aura of power and authority but never really wanted to dominate Tess nor did he abuse her, yet trying to break her just to keep his demon lurked in the dark pit of his life. Tess is not submissive by nature instead she has her own dark twisted fantasy which she never releases until Q unlocks it. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Only think of me and what I’m doing. There is intimacy in pain esclave. Let me make your pain my pleasure.” </i>
</b><br><br>But when time comes for her let go this twisted reality will she embrace her freedom? Or will she go back to her master the one her body obeys?<br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410975340i/11178203._SX540_.jpg" width="450" height="330" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved the strength Tess carried throughout the book, Loved her transition from timid girl to a fighter, to a strong woman who embraced her true desire. I loved the passion and growing intensity between them. This is one unconventional love story, living together they didn't fix each other but unleashed their darkness to heal them both. <br><br><b>
  <i>“I’m willing to be your monster Q.”</i>
</b><br><br>The epilogue in Q’s POV was beautiful you will see his horrid past in bits and pieces. Once you learn them you will definitely fall for Q, there is more to him than just a monster.<br> <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="6112273930878068998" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18399439-tears-of-tess">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=i-like-it-dark-and-twisted">i-like-it-dark-and-twisted</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer830732435" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13594506565831773614"><b>3.75 ~ 4 Stars </b> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390493642i/8230798._SY540_.jpg' width='380' height='440' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I really enjoyed Pepper Winters’ writing and I think she is very talented. She has a really nice flow that made the story line work.<br/><br/>We are once again kidnapped in Mexico and fall into the seedy world of human trafficking. Seriously, I may never go to Mexico after all these types of books.<br/><br/>Tess, the main character really drives the message to a reader that she is not satisfied with her sex life with her longtime boyfriend, Brax. I mean the author makes this very clear that Tess wan</span>
  <span id="freeText13594506565831773614" style="display:none"><b>3.75 ~ 4 Stars </b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390493642i/8230798._SY540_.jpg" width="380" height="440" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I really enjoyed Pepper Winters’ writing and I think she is very talented. She has a really nice flow that made the story line work.<br><br>We are once again kidnapped in Mexico and fall into the seedy world of human trafficking. Seriously, I may never go to Mexico after all these types of books.<br><br>Tess, the main character really drives the message to a reader that she is not satisfied with her sex life with her longtime boyfriend, Brax. I mean the author makes this very clear that Tess wants kinky and is drawn to a submissive role in the bedroom and Brax isn’t interested at all.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>I mean come on Brax!<br><br>Tess finds herself captured and in an outfit out of Flashdance at the hands of monsters and is sold. Of course in the back of a readers mind your thinking well she should like this but what she yearns for is kink with the safety and embrace of love.<br><br><b>
  <i>"Why did you buy me?" He leaned back, steepling his fingers.<br><br>"I didn't. You were a gift. An unwanted gift." His lips twitched. <br><br>"A bribe, if you will."</i>
</b><br><br>Tess was hard to like for the majority of the book because her emotions were ALL over the map, she likes him, she hates him, she wants to go home, etc. She was a bit exhausting but in the end I appreciated her making up her mind and going for it!<br><br>Q isn’t what he seems and then again he is. I found his portion of the story interesting and I will continue on to the sequel to see where these two BIRDS will go from here.<br><br>Together they make perfect sense...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390498146ra/8232572.gif" width="380" height="320" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"Only think of me and what I'm doing. There is intimacy in pain, esclave. Let me make your pain my pleasure." </i>
</b><br><br>Some things didn’t really work for me in the story but overall, this was a good read and it did hold my attention so onto the next book.<br><br><b>
  <i>"I want to hurt you. I want to own you. I want to devour you. I want to make you mine. I'm already yours." </i>
</b><br><br>P.S. Doesn't end with a cliffhanger- always a plus!<br></span>

<div id="review_669215146" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/669215146" />
    <a title="Didi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6082482-didi"><img alt="Didi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459297426p2/6082482.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/669215146?book_show_action=true">Jul 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Didi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Didi" href="/user/show/6082482-didi">Didi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">lovers of dark and gritty romance</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=unable-to-put-down">unable-to-put-down</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=second-chances">second-chances</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=bdsm">bdsm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=abused-woman">abused-woman</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=billionairre-alpha-male">billionairre-alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=hot-as-hell">hot-as-hell</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=my-captor-lover">my-captor-lover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=kidnapping">kidnapping</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer669215146" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15304548343194433422">********** 4.5 STARS!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!! ************<br/><br/>HOLY MOTHER OF ALL THINGS HOLY!<br/><br/>THIS WAS BY FAR THE DARKEST, MOST PROVOCATIVE, MOST CONTROVERSIAL BOOK IN ITS GENRE!<br/><br/>AND I LOVED IT.<br/><br/>Tears of Tess is not your average captor tale. It's not your average dark romance with a redeemable hero. It's not your average heroine being rescued by her meant to be.<br/><br/>it is:<br/>RAW<br/>EDGY<br/>DARK<br/>DISTURBING<br/>HORRIFIC<br/>SCANDALOUS<br/>BRUTAL<br/>UNFORGIVING<br/><br/>AND I LOVED EVERY SECOND, MINUTE, HOUR, DAY, IT TOOK TO READ IT.<br/><br/>Tess Winters is a 2</span>
  <span id="freeText15304548343194433422" style="display:none">********** 4.5 STARS!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!! ************<br /><br />HOLY MOTHER OF ALL THINGS HOLY!<br /><br />THIS WAS BY FAR THE DARKEST, MOST PROVOCATIVE, MOST CONTROVERSIAL BOOK IN ITS GENRE!<br /><br />AND I LOVED IT.<br /><br />Tears of Tess is not your average captor tale. It's not your average dark romance with a redeemable hero. It's not your average heroine being rescued by her meant to be.<br /><br />it is:<br />RAW<br />EDGY<br />DARK<br />DISTURBING<br />HORRIFIC<br />SCANDALOUS<br />BRUTAL<br />UNFORGIVING<br /><br />AND I LOVED EVERY SECOND, MINUTE, HOUR, DAY, IT TOOK TO READ IT.<br /><br />Tess Winters is a 20 year old woman on the verge of creating her own wonderful life. She's almost done university and looking forward to the life she's building with her boyfriend of 2 years, Brax Cliffingstone. <br /><br />As a celebration, Brax whisks Tess off to Cancun, Mexico for a vacation. It's meant to help them re-connect and re-claim the intimacy that has taken second place to the urgencies of life.<br /><br />But soon into their tropical paradise Tess is kidnapped. She is bought and sold to the highest bidder. She is brutalized and beaten into submission----BUT IS SHE?<br /><br />I won't go into the details of her capture or what happens at the hands of her kidnappers because it should be read and felt--and you will feel--but her life truly takes a turn when she is sold to the dark and mysterious Q.<br /><br />And holy shit things take off. like fireworks!!!<br /><br />This is not a romance veiled as dark and redeemable. This is truly an abrasive, horrifying look at the sex trade industry and the depths of it's success. This fact isn't thrown into your face as a type of soap box, but it's woven into the story so well that you end up learning as much as being reluctantly entertained.<br /><br />I can't stress how vicious and dark this is. It's not for the faint of heart or those against forced seduction. But it is:<br /><br />RELENTLESS IN IT'S BRUTALITY AS Q IS IN TAKING HIS SUBMISSION FROM TESS.<br /><br />The darkness isn't held back. Pepper Winter's writes with an incredibly primal and unapologetic way. And I couldn't put it down!<br /><br />Q is the ultimate anti-hero. He knows he has issues that surpass any psychiatric evaluation. He knows his darkness is waiting to consume him, take over the fraility of his hard earned control. But Tess, she changes everything and brings the beast to life.<br />And Q is a beast--in all forms, sexually, physically and emotionally!<br />The man is in a class of his own. Q you are ah-maz-ing!<br /><br />Is Q redeemable? is Tess who she thinks she is? Is she repressing a darkness only challenged by Q? Is she ready to accept who she possibly can be?<br /><br />It's beautiful to watch Tess transform from helpless victim to bona fide fighter. She is given no choice, but when faced with death she rises to the challenge and proves she's worthy of respect.<br />I liked Tess but the reason I'm giving this book 4.5 stars is because her strength, although commendable was sometimes unrealistic.<br /><br />She did things that where unlikely. I understood her desire to fight and not be taken down but I think most people in similar situations would be horrified to inaction.<br /><br />Regardless, she really blossomed and grew into the best version of herself.<br /><br />But her and Q together...HOLY, HOLY, HOLY! There are scenes in this book that left me speechless, breathless...holy shit.<br /><br />I can't say anymore because there is so, so, so much that goes on here that by the time I finished I felt like I had been on a journey. I could not put this down. <br /><br />INCREDIBLE. HORRIFIC. BRUTAL. BEAUTIFUL.<br />LOVED IT.<br /><br />Genre: Erotic romance/BDSM<br />Steam: OFF THE CHARTS, GRAB A FIRE EXTINGUISHER!<br />Pov: 1st person- Tess, last chapter and epilogue 1st person- Q<br />Cliffy: A dark HEA...<br /><br />**ARC KINDLY PROVIDED BY THE AUTHOR FOR AN HONEST REVIEW.**<br /><br />FOR A LOOK AT THE TRAILER FOR THIS BOOK, PLEASE VISIT:<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZI1azW2ydUo&amp;feature=youtu.be">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZI1azW...</a><br /><br />Original review posted at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.choicebookreviews.net">www.choicebookreviews.net</a><br /><br />RELEASE DATE: SEPTEMBER 6, 2013.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15304548343194433422" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer15648546788048755068"><br/><b>***4 Stars***</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>Three words.<br/><br/>I was sold.</b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Dark and Gritty. It was everything I expected, yet not at all. <br/><br/>Tess was a girl who craved acceptance, yearned to belong and ached to feel passion; living a settled and monotonous life with her boyfriend, yet lonely and wanting more. One bad decision thrust her into a nightmare, and in the darkness she found a monster...her monster.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395156ra/760998.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Q was a man wrestling with demons. Fighting urges and cravings that lived in the darkest part of his soul. Somehow Tess’s spiri</span>
  <span id="freeText15648546788048755068" style="display:none"><br><b>***4 Stars***</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>Three words.<br><br>I was sold.</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Dark and Gritty. It was everything I expected, yet not at all. <br><br>Tess was a girl who craved acceptance, yearned to belong and ached to feel passion; living a settled and monotonous life with her boyfriend, yet lonely and wanting more. One bad decision thrust her into a nightmare, and in the darkness she found a monster...her monster.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395156ra/760998.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Q was a man wrestling with demons. Fighting urges and cravings that lived in the darkest part of his soul. Somehow Tess’s spirit and passion called to that darkness.   <b>"I'm not afraid of hurting you. I'm afraid of how far I'm willing to go."<b></b></b>

The physical is obvious, but it’s what’s bubbling underneath that draws you in and keeps you captive. I will admit that at times it was difficult to read. Situations that were told in such graphic detail, your breathing quickened and palms ached from squeezing your kindle in order to bear the actions.<br> <br>Be prepared to feel an array of emotions, springboarding from one to the next. From joy to sadness. Grief to anger. Desperation to perversion. It’s all there...living and breathing in an isolated French mansion. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396665992i/9170309.jpg" width="540" height="340" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380378870i/734719.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14144676-sammy?shelf=alpha-goodness">alpha-goodness</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14144676-sammy?shelf=dark-and-twisted">dark-and-twisted</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1035809677" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15628076978412848465">Rating: 4.5 ★'s<br/><br/>Whenever I see friends giving out recommendations for dark reads, Pepper Winter's Monsters in the Dark series is always on the list.<br/><br/>Dark.<br/><br/>Gritty.<br/><br/>Intense.<br/><br/>Deliciously Twisted.<br/><br/>Words that I have seen commonly used to describe this series and after reading Tears of Tess, I couldn't agree with them more! Seriously, why did I wait so long to start this series!?! I was consumed by this story, anxious to see what was in store for Tess, intrigued by the mysterious Q, and unable to put this b</span>
  <span id="freeText15628076978412848465" style="display:none">Rating: 4.5 ★'s<br><br>Whenever I see friends giving out recommendations for dark reads, Pepper Winter's Monsters in the Dark series is always on the list.<br><br>Dark.<br><br>Gritty.<br><br>Intense.<br><br>Deliciously Twisted.<br><br>Words that I have seen commonly used to describe this series and after reading Tears of Tess, I couldn't agree with them more! Seriously, why did I wait so long to start this series!?! I was consumed by this story, anxious to see what was in store for Tess, intrigued by the mysterious Q, and unable to put this book down!<br><br><b>"Three little words that terrified, stole my breath, and made my life flicker before my eyes. <br><br>Three little words.<br><br>I was sold."</b><br><br>What happens when you are ripped away from the only happiness you have ever known? Abducted, drugged, and sold as a slave with the expectation that you will give up everything about yourself to become what your new master wants you to be? This is the nightmare that Tess Snow finds herself in when she is taken while on vacation with her boyfriend in Mexico.<br><br>*~*~*~*~*<br><br><b>FIGHTER.</b> If I had to describe Tess with one word, that would be my choice. With her boyfriend Brax, Tess was somewhat of a push-over but following her abduction, she evolved into a warrior and refused to be broken by her captors. I really respected how she kept certain aspects of herself private, the consequences of keeping those secrets be damned. The only minor frustration that I experienced with Tess' character stemmed from her capricious decision making; one moment she would decide to do one thing and then in the next instant she would do the exact opposite.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412438286i/11375767._SY540_.jpg" height="375" width="375" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My word choice for Q (Tess' Master) would be <b>ENIGMA.</b> Throughout most of this book, Q was a complete mystery to me. He's kind of like a complex puzzle. I would analyze his words and actions for clues and try to piece them together to see what his true motivations were. I wanted to know if there was more to him than the calculating, ruthless, and demanding man that he was around Tess.<br><br>*~*~*~*~*<br><br>Tears of Tess is definitely a <b>dark read</b> and <b>not for the faint of heart.</b> There were moments in this book where I was cringing, my heart was racing because I was so nervous for Tess, and I kept thinking "No! This can't be happening!" My dark romance boundaries were pushed, that's for sure =) To be honest, I am a tad bit nervous about starting Quintessentially Q (#2) because I've heard that the dark scenes are even more intense, but I will be reading it ASAP because I NEED to know what is in store for Tess and Q next!<br><br>*~*~*~*~*<br><br>Tears of Tess is a captivating story about a woman discovering her inner strength in the most unexpected of ways. Learning to not only face her inner demons, but to embrace them as a means of finding self acceptance. It's a story about love. Finding that person that makes her feel complete despite her flaws and imperfections.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15628076978412848465" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('VQRQKi495o692VtfsnmndapYvIUDZVE3Fmd55Oxkerc4bH09IPfmoYoSEt4V53D6kqUdi5tDyLxGTxAt8IJQpw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('flfQbn0R+tGVcOgHTs3jY+S/O/ApAN5y1j4S8QwKz+ETP/15c9v6/qK7oYbpUzTs3EKa/rEmR/mGFns4EOzl8Q==')})
  }

Kidnapped as a young boy and sold into slavery by a power-hungry mobster, he has thought of nothing but vengeance. For twelve years he has immersed himself in the world of pleasure slaves searching <\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText15185835480987712505\" style=\"display:none\">Caleb is a man with a singular interest in revenge. Kidnapped as a young boy and sold into slavery by a power-hungry mobster, he has thought of nothing but vengeance. For twelve years he has immersed himself in the world of pleasure slaves searching for the one man he holds ultimately responsible. Finally, the architect of his suffering has emerged with a new identity, but not a new nature. If Caleb is to get close enough to strike, he must become the very thing he abhors and kidnap a beautiful girl to train her to be all that he once was.\n\nEighteen-year-old Olivia Ruiz has just woken up in a strange place. Blindfolded and bound, there is only a calm male voice to welcome her. His name is Caleb, though he demands to be called Master. Olivia is young, beautiful, naïve and willful to a fault. She has a dark sensuality that cannot be hidden or denied, though she tries to accomplish both. Although she is frightened by the strong, sadistic, and arrogant man who holds her prisoner, what keeps Olivia awake in the dark is her unwelcome attraction to him.\n\nWARNING: This book contains very   <span id="freeText11485400890578111151" style="display:none">Pepper Winters is a multiple New York Times, Wall Street Journal, and USA Today International Bestseller.<br /><br />She currently has thirty books released in nine languages. She’s hit best-seller lists (USA Today, New York Times, and Wall Street Journal) thirty-three times. She dabbles in multiple genres, ranging from Dark Romance to Coming of Age. <br /><br />After chasing her dreams to become a full-time writer, Pepper has earned recognition with awards for best Dark Romance, best BDSM Series, and best Hero. She’s an multiple #1 iBooks bestseller, along with #1 in Erotic Romance, Romantic Suspense, Contemporary, and Erotica Thriller. With 20 books currently published, she has hit the bestseller charts twenty-nine times in three years. <br /><br />Pepper is a Hybrid Author of both Traditional and Self-published work. Her Pure Corruption Series was released by Grand Central, Hachette.<br /><br />Her books have garnered foreign interest and are currently being translated into numerous languages, including already released titles in Italian, French, Hebrew, German, and Turkish. <br /><br />NEWSLETTER: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.subscribepage.com/www.pepperwinters.com">http://www.subscribepage.com/www.pepp...</a><br /><br />Or follow her on her website<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.pepperwinters.com">www.pepperwinters.com</a><br /><br />She loves mail of any kind: pepperwinters@gmail.com<br /><br />You can stalk her here:<br /><br />Pinterest/Pepperwinters<br />Facebook Pepper Winters<br />Twitter @pepperwinters<br />Blog pepperwinters.wordpress.com</span>
